[30;1m117 | [0m[35m## Version-String Flavors[0m
[30;1m118 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m119 | [0m[35mCode which uses Versioneer can learn about its version string at runtime by[0m
[30;1m120 | [0m[35mimporting `_version` from your main `__init__.py` file and running the[0m

[30;1m97 | [0m[35mVersioneer works by adding a special `_version.py` file into your source[0m
[30;1m98 | [0m[35mtree, where your `__init__.py` can import it. This `_version.py` knows how to[0m
[30;1m99 | [0m[35mdynamically ask the VCS tool for version information at import time.[0m
[30;1m100 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m102 | [0m[35mprocess marks `_version.py` to have this marker rewritten with a tag name[0m
